# Benchmark Results — 3-way on local qwen (codex · qclaude 122b · qclaude35 35b)

- **Tools & models:**
  - `codex` (Codex CLI) → `qwen-122b-codex` — **122b**
  - `qclaude` (Claude Code, `--model opus`) → `qwen-122b-claude` — **122b** (same weights as codex)
  - `qclaude35` (Claude Code, `--model sonnet`) → `qwen-35b-claude` — **35b** (the fast tier)
- **What each axis isolates:**
  - **codex vs qclaude** = same 122b weights, different client/agent-loop (Codex Responses→chat vs Claude Code Anthropic→chat).
  - **qclaude vs qclaude35** = same client (Claude Code), different model size (122b vs 35b).
- All three: same frozen `tasks/<level>/PROMPT.md`, same isolated-run harness (`benchmark/run.sh`), same independent judges (`tasks/<level>/test.py`). All qwen served through role-shim → mlx (122b :8001 / 35b :8000).
- **Levels:** 7 (L1–L7).

> Durable record: `benchmark/.runs/` is gitignored — the table + excerpts below are the committed evidence.

### Scoreboard

| Tool | Passed | Total wall-clock |
|------|--------|------------------|
| codex (122b) | 5/7 | 484s |
| qclaude (122b/opus) | 6/7 | 2028s |
| qclaude35 (35b/sonnet) | 6/7 | 949s |

### Reading the numbers

- **Success** = each level's independent black-box judge (`tasks/<level>/test.py`) re-run against the produced files. Never the tool's self-report.
- **Steps use different units** — codex = `exec` blocks; qclaude/qclaude35 = `tool_use` events in the stream-json transcript. Compare shape, not integers.
- **Time is dominated by cold prefill of a large prompt — not by the model and not by 'caching'.** codex also runs on local mlx (no Anthropic caching either). Claude Code just sends a much larger prompt (system prompt + ~25 tool schemas + skills), and mlx re-prefills it cold every task (per-task time-to-first-token 79–196s here). Prefill is linear (~1.75s/1k tokens on this 122b). 35b being faster than 122b is a real model-size effect. See finding 5 below for the full measurement and levers.
- **Size** = files + LOC produced, excluding harness artifacts.

### Findings & honesty (read this)

Headline pass counts: **codex 5/7 · qclaude(122b) 6/7 · qclaude35(35b) 6/7.** But the
*kinds* of failure are the story — each isolates a different variable.

1. **L3-kvstore — agent-loop, not model (codex FAIL, both Claude Code PASS).** codex's L3
   is a model-loop degeneration: first action `mkdir -p kvstore` (empty stdout), then
   qwen-122b re-emits its preamble with no tool call and `codex exec` exits clean with
   **0 files**. The *identical 122b weights* under Claude Code completed the package
   (9f/376loc), and even **35b** completed it (8f/230loc). So L3 is a Codex agent-loop
   failure, not a model-capability one.

2. **L4-calc — the one clean model-size signal (122b PASS, 35b FAIL).** Both 122b runs
   (codex and qclaude) pass. **35b fails**: its calculator accepts the invalid expression
   `2 3` (two numbers, no operator) and exits 0 instead of erroring
   (`FAIL l4-calc: invalid expr '2 3' exited 0 (want nonzero)`). This is a real
   error-handling gap the larger model catches — the place where 122b earns its cost.

3. **L7-kvapi — layout variance, disclosed (codex FAIL, qclaude FAIL, qclaude35 PASS).**
   - **codex**: same degeneration as L3 — built **0 files**.
   - **qclaude(122b)**: built a *working* service (its own pytest: **18/18 functional
     tests pass**) but nested everything under a `solution/` subdir; the frozen contract's
     judge wants `serve.py` at the run-dir **root**, so it scores FAIL on layout, not
     function.
   - **qclaude35(35b)**: built the same service with `serve.py` at the **root** → judge
     PASS. This cross-confirms that qclaude(122b)'s L7 FAIL was a layout-choice variance,
     not an inability to build the service.

4. **Speed — 35b is ~1.5–3.4× faster than 122b** under the same client (e.g. L3 103s vs
   351s, L5 121s vs 342s) — a real model-size effect (smaller model prefills and generates
   faster).
5. **Why both qclaude runs are slower than codex — measured, and it is NOT "caching".**
   codex also runs against the same local mlx, so it gets no Anthropic prompt caching
   either. The real cause is **prompt size × cold prefill**: Claude Code sends a very large
   prompt (system prompt + ~25 tool schemas + skills/agents), and mlx re-prefills it cold
   on **every task** — per-task time-to-first-token was **79–196s** (40–60% of each task's
   wall-clock), i.e. the giant prompt is processed before any output. Prefill is linear on
   this 122b (~1.75s per 1k prompt tokens; 16k tok → 28s, measured). mlx's prompt cache
   (on by default, size 10) reuses an *identical* prefix in ~0.1s (measured), but across
   the 7 separate tasks the static system-prompt prefix is not reused (per-task cwd/session
   content near the top breaks the common prefix), so each task pays the full cold prefill.
   codex's prompts are much smaller, so its prefill — and total time — is far lower.
   Levers to close the gap: shrink Claude Code's prompt (fewer tools/skills/plugins/MCP),
   prefer the 35b tier, and size `--prompt-cache-*` so the static prefix survives.
6. **Two levers measured.** (a) **Shrinking the prompt works, dramatically.** Re-running
   L1 on the same 122b with `--bare --tools Write Edit Read Bash --disable-slash-commands`
   (3 tool schemas instead of 25, no CLAUDE.md/memory/skills injection) cut
   **time-to-first-token 98.6s → 8.9s (11×)** and **total 158s → 28.5s (5.5×)**, still
   PASS — i.e. down to codex-class speed (~23s). This is the highest-leverage fix and
   confirms the prompt size, not the model, was the cost. (b) **`--prefill-step-size` does
   not help:** bumping the mlx server 2048 → 8192 left a fresh 20k-token cold prefill
   unchanged (37.7s → 39.4s, within noise) — the prefill bottleneck is compute, not batch
   step size. Reverted.

**Bottom line.** For these small, well-specified tasks the **35b (qclaude35) is a strong,
much faster default** — 6/7, failing only one corner error-case — while the **122b buys
that corner back** (calc error handling). codex's 5/7 is held down by agent-loop
degeneration (L3/L7), not by the model, which is the same 122b qclaude runs.

### qclaude35 / l1-fib — PASS in 69s

-- set / get ---------------------------------------------------------\n\n    def test_set_and_get(self) -> None:\n        self._run(\"set\", \"foo\", \"bar\")\n        out = self._run(\"get\", \"foo\")\n        self.assertEqual(out.stdout.strip(), \"bar\")\n\n    def test_get_missing_key(self) -> None:\n        out = self._run(\"get\", \"nope\", expect_returncode=1)\n        self.assertEqual(out.stdout, \"\")\n\n    def test_overwrite_value(self) -> None:\n        self._run(\"set\", \"k\", \"v1\")\n        self._run(\"set\", \"k\", \"v2\")\n        out = self._run(\"get\", \"k\")\n        self.assertEqual(out.stdout.strip(), \"v2\")\n\n    # -- delete ------------------------------------------------------------\n\n    def test_delete_existing(self) -> None:\n        self._run(\"set\", \"k\", \"v\")\n        self._run(\"delete\", \"k\")\n        out = self._run(\"get\", \"k\", expect_returncode=1)\n        self.assertEqual(out.stdout, \"\")\n\n    def test_delete_missing_is_idempotent(self) -> None:\n        self._run(\"delete\", \"nope\")  # should exit 0\n\n    # -- list --------------------------------------------------------------\n\n    def test_list_empty(self) -> None:\n        out = self._run(\"list\")\n        self.assertEqual(out.stdout, \"\")\n\n    def test_list_sorted(self) -> None:\n        for k, v in [(\"charlie\", \"3\"), (\"alpha\", \"1\"), (\"beta\", \"2\")]:\n            self._run(\"set\", k, v)\n        out = self._run(\"list\")\n        self.assertEqual(out.stdout.strip(), \"alpha\\nbeta\\ncharlie\")\n\n    # -- persistence across processes --------------------------------------\n\n    def test_persistence(self) -> None:\n        self._run(\"set\", \"persist\", \"yes\")\n        # separate process invocation\n        out = subprocess.run([*CLI, \"get\", \"persist\"],\n                             capture_output=True, text=True, env=self.env)\n        self.assertEqual(out.returncode, 0)\n        self.assertEqual(out.stdout.strip(), \"yes\")\n\n\nclass KVStoreUnitTestCase(unittest.TestCase):\n    \"\"\"Unit tests for the KVStore class directly.\"\"\"\n\n    def setUp(self) -> None:\n        self.tmpdir = tempfile.mkdtemp()\n        self.store_path = Path(self.tmpdir) / \"unit.db\"\n\n    def test_get_returns_none_for_missing(self) -> None:\n        from kvstore import KVStore\n        store = KVStore(path=str(self.store_path))\n        self.assertIsNone(store.get(\"missing\"))\n\n    def test_keys_sorted(self) -> None:\n        from kvstore import KVStore\n        store = KVStore(path=str(self.store_path))\n        store.set(\"z\", \"1\")\n        store.set(\"a\", \"2\")\n        store.set(\"m\", \"3\")\n        self.assertEqual(store.keys(), [\"a\", \"m\", \"z\"])\n\n    def test_delete_removes_key(self) -> None:\n        from kvstore import KVStore\n        store = KVStore(path=str(self.store_path))\n        store.set(\"k\", \"v\")\n        store.delete(\"k\")\n        self.assertIsNone(store.get(\"k\"))\n\n\nif __name__ == \"__main__\":\n    unittest.main()\n"},"name":"Write","type":"tool_use"}],"id":"msg_1782791062769264000","model":"qwen-35b-claude","role":"assistant","stop_reason":null,"stop_sequence":null,"type":"message","usage":{"cache_creation":{"ephemeral_1h_input_tokens":0,"ephemeral_5m_input_tokens":0},"cache_creation_input_tokens":0,"cache_read_input_tokens":0,"input_tokens":0,"output_tokens":0},"context_management":null},"parent_tool_use_id":null,"session_id":"fd53d1ee-a527-48d6-bb17-73ac1a76dfa0","uuid":"52c926b0-ec68-4541-a4cf-10e631f360e8"}

Find column index\n    if col_name not in headers:\n        print(f\"Error: column '{col_name}' not found\", file=sys.stderr)\n        sys.exit(1)\n\n    col_idx = headers.index(col_name)\n\n    # Extract numeric values\n    values = []\n    for row in rows:\n        if col_idx >= len(row):\n            print(f\"Error: missing value in column '{col_name}'\", file=sys.stderr)\n            sys.exit(1)\n        try:\n            values.append(float(row[col_idx]))\n        except ValueError:\n            print(f\"Error: column '{col_name}' is not numeric\", file=sys.stderr)\n            sys.exit(1)\n\n    stats = compute_stats(values)\n\n    print(f\"count: {stats['count']}\")\n    print(f\"min: {fmt(stats['min'])}\")\n    print(f\"max: {fmt(stats['max'])}\")\n    print(f\"sum: {fmt(stats['sum'])}\")\n    print(f\"mean: {fmt(stats['mean'])}\")\n\n\ndef main():\n    if len(sys.argv) < 2:\n        print(\"Usage: python3 csvstat.py <file.csv> --cols | --col <name>\", file=sys.stderr)\n        sys.exit(1)\n\n    filepath = sys.argv[1]\n\n    if \"--cols\" in sys.argv:\n        list_columns(filepath)\n    elif \"--col\" in sys.argv:\n        if len(sys.argv) < 4:\n            print(\"Usage: python3 csvstat.py <file.csv> --col <name>\", file=sys.stderr)\n            sys.exit(1)\n        col_name = sys.argv[3]\n        column_stats(filepath, col_name)\n    else:\n        print(\"Usage: python3 csvstat.py <file.csv> --cols | --col <name>\", file=sys.stderr)\n        sys.exit(1)\n\n\nif __name__ == \"__main__\":\n    main()\n","structuredPatch":[],"originalFile":null,"userModified":false}}

class-level, set by server\n\n    # -- routing -----------------------------------------------------------\n\n    def _route(self, method: str) -> None:\n        path = self.path\n        m = re.fullmatch(r\"/kv/([^/]+)\", path)\n        if m:\n            key = m.group(1)\n            getattr(self, f\"_handle_{method}_{key}\")()\n        elif path == \"/kv\":\n            getattr(self, f\"_handle_{method}\")()\n        else:\n            self._send_error(404, \"not found\")\n\n    def do_GET(self) -> None:\n        self._route(\"GET\")\n\n    def do_PUT(self) -> None:\n        self._route(\"PUT\")\n\n    def do_DELETE(self) -> None:\n        self._route(\"DELETE\")\n\n    # -- key operations ----------------------------------------------------\n\n    def _handle_GET_key(self) -> None:\n        val = self._store.get(self._key)\n        if val is None:\n            self._send_error(404, \"key not found\")\n        else:\n            self._send_response(200, val)\n\n    def _handle_PUT_key(self) -> None:\n        body = self._read_body()\n        self._store.put(self._key, body)\n        self._send_response(200, \"\")\n\n    def _handle_DELETE_key(self) -> None:\n        if self._store.delete(self._key):\n            self._send_response(200, \"\")\n        else:\n            self._send_error(404, \"key not found\")\n\n    # -- collection operations ---------------------------------------------\n\n    def _handle_GET(self) -> None:\n        keys = self._store.keys()\n        self._send_response(200, json.dumps(keys), \"application/json\")\n\n    # -- helpers -----------------------------------------------------------\n\n    @property\n    def _key(self) -> str:\n        # re.fullmatch already captured it; strip the leading /kv/\n        return self.path.split(\"/kv/\", 1)[1]\n\n    def _read_body(self) -> str:\n        length = int(self.headers.get(\"Content-Length\", 0))\n        return self.rfile.read(length).decode(\"utf-8\")\n\n    def _send_response(self, code: int, body: str, mime: str = \"text/plain\") -> None:\n        self.send_response(code)\n        self.send_header(\"Content-Type\", mime)\n        self.send_header(\"Content-Length\", str(len(body.encode(\"utf-8\"))))\n        self.end_headers()\n        self.wfile.write(body.encode(\"utf-8\"))\n\n    def _send_error(self, code: int, reason: str) -> None:\n        self.send_response(code)\n        self.send_header(\"Content-Length\", str(len(reason)))\n        self.end_headers()\n        self.wfile.write(reason.encode(\"utf-8\"))\n\n    # -- silence per-request logs ------------------------------------------\n\n    def log_message(self, fmt: str, *args: object) -> None:\n        pass\n\n\ndef main() -> None:\n    parser = argparse.ArgumentParser(description=\"KV API server\")\n    parser.add_argument(\"--port\", type=int, default=8080)\n    args = parser.parse_args()\n\n    store = Store()\n    Handler._store = store\n\n    server = HTTPServer((\"127.0.0.1\", args.port), Handler)\n    try:\n        server.serve_forever()\n    except KeyboardInterrupt:\n        pass\n    finally:\n        server.server_close()\n\n\nif __name__ == \"__main__\":\n    main()\n"},"name":"Write","type":"tool_use"}],"id":"msg_1782791474470099000","model":"qwen-35b-claude","role":"assistant","stop_reason":null,"stop_sequence":null,"type":"message","usage":{"cache_creation":{"ephemeral_1h_input_tokens":0,"ephemeral_5m_input_tokens":0},"cache_creation_input_tokens":0,"cache_read_input_tokens":0,"input_tokens":0,"output_tokens":0},"context_management":null},"parent_tool_use_id":null,"session_id":"3c03db94-f643-4e3f-8d27-522a1f5abf1f","uuid":"b98b0206-5e9d-4840-a039-f798f3cc8511"}

{"type":"assistant","message":{"content":[{"id":"6dcb75a5-d1ec-4797-99cc-b4955f1e7c10","input":{"file_path":"/Users/ohama/projs/codex/benchmark/.runs/qclaude35-l7-kvapi-20260630-035038/kvapi/storage.py","content":"\"\"\"Persistent key-value store backed by a JSON file.\"\"\"\n\nimport json\nimport os\nfrom pathlib import Path\n\n\nclass Store:\n    \"\"\"Thread-safe-ish JSON-file KV store.\n\n    Keys and values are plain UTF-8 strings. The entire store is loaded into\n    memory on init and written back on every mutation.\n    \"\"\"\n\n    def __init__(self, path: str | None = None) -> None:\n        self._path = Path(path or os.environ.get(\"KVAPI_PATH\", \"./kvapi.db\"))\n        self._data: dict[str, str] = {}\n        self._load()\n\n    # -- public API --------------------------------------------------------\n\n    def get(self, key: str) -> str | None:\n        return self._data.get(key)\n\n    def put(self, key: str, value: str) -> None:\n        self._data[key] = value\n        self._save()\n\n    def delete(self, key: str) -> bool:\n        if key not in self._data:\n            return False\n        del self._data[key]\n        self._save()\n        return True\n\n    def keys(self) -> list[str]:\n        return sorted(self._data)\n\n    # -- internals ---------------------------------------------------------\n\n    def _load(self) -> None:\n        if not self._path.exists():\n            return\n        with open(self._path, \"r\", encoding=\"utf-8\") as f:\n            self._data = json.load(f)\n\n    def _save(self) -> None:\n        with open(self._path, \"w\", encoding=\"utf-8\") as f:\n            json.dump(self._data, f, ensure_ascii=False)\n"},"name":"Write","type":"tool_use"}],"id":"msg_1782791474470099000","model":"qwen-35b-claude","role":"assistant","stop_reason":null,"stop_sequence":null,"type":"message","usage":{"cache_creation":{"ephemeral_1h_input_tokens":0,"ephemeral_5m_input_tokens":0},"cache_creation_input_tokens":0,"cache_read_input_tokens":0,"input_tokens":0,"output_tokens":0},"context_management":null},"parent_tool_use_id":null,"session_id":"3c03db94-f643-4e3f-8d27-522a1f5abf1f","uuid":"961d3124-58e7-4b6b-84cd-5f3fb764ef9f"}

The entire store is loaded into\n    memory on init and written back on every mutation.\n    \"\"\"\n\n    def __init__(self, path: str | None = None) -> None:\n        self._path = Path(path or os.environ.get(\"KVAPI_PATH\", \"./kvapi.db\"))\n        self._data: dict[str, str] = {}\n        self._load()\n\n    # -- public API --------------------------------------------------------\n\n    def get(self, key: str) -> str | None:\n        return self._data.get(key)\n\n    def put(self, key: str, value: str) -> None:\n        self._data[key] = value\n        self._save()\n\n    def delete(self, key: str) -> bool:\n        if key not in self._data:\n            return False\n        del self._data[key]\n        self._save()\n        return True\n\n    def keys(self) -> list[str]:\n        return sorted(self._data)\n\n    # -- internals ---------------------------------------------------------\n\n    def _load(self) -> None:\n        if not self._path.exists():\n            return\n        with open(self._path, \"r\", encoding=\"utf-8\") as f:\n            self._data = json.load(f)\n\n    def _save(self) -> None:\n        with open(self._path, \"w\", encoding=\"utf-8\") as f:\n            json.dump(self._data, f, ensure_ascii=False)\n","structuredPatch":[],"originalFile":null,"userModified":false}}
